### Assistant

Perfect! Now I can see the issue. The network detection script has a global variable `isCorporateNetworkDetected` that tracks the corporate network status, but the corporate content loader is not checking this variable before loading content.

The key issue is that the corporate content loader's auto-loading logic in the `DOMContentLoaded` event handler (lines 884-904 in corporate-content-loader.js) doesn't respect the network detection results. It just checks if the page needs corporate content and then loads it regardless of network status.

Let me fix this by modifying the corporate content loader to respect the network detection:

### Assistant

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/q284340/Agentic/nano-degree/docs-content/javascripts/corporate-content-loader.js",
  "old_string": "    // Auto-load corporate content when needed\n    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {\n        console.log('🔐 Corporate content loader initialized');\n        \n        // Check if current page needs corporate content\n        if (window.CorporateContentLoader.isCorporateContentNeeded()) {\n            console.log('🔐 Page needs corporate content, attempting to load...');\n            \n            try {\n                const loaded = await window.CorporateContentLoader.load();\n                if (loaded) {\n                    console.log('✅ Corporate content loaded successfully');\n                } else {\n                    console.log('❌ Corporate content loading failed or content not available');\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error('❌ Error loading corporate content:', error);\n            }\n        } else {\n            console.log('🔐 Page does not need corporate content');\n        }",
  "new_string": "    // Auto-load corporate content when needed and authorized\n    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {\n        console.log('🔐 Corporate content loader initialized');\n        \n        // Check if current page needs corporate content\n        if (window.CorporateContentLoader.isCorporateContentNeeded()) {\n            console.log('🔐 Page needs corporate content, checking network authorization...');\n            \n            // Wait a bit for network detection to complete\n            setTimeout(async () => {\n                // Check if network detection has authorized corporate content access\n                // This checks the global variable set by network-detection.js\n                const isAuthorized = window.isCorporateNetworkDetected || \n                                   (typeof isCorporateNetworkDetected !== 'undefined' && isCorporateNetworkDetected);\n                \n                if (isAuthorized) {\n                    console.log('✅ Corporate network detected - loading corporate content');\n                    try {\n                        const loaded = await window.CorporateContentLoader.load();\n                        if (loaded) {\n                            console.log('✅ Corporate content loaded successfully');\n                        } else {\n                            console.log('❌ Corporate content loading failed or content not available');\n                        }\n                    } catch (error) {\n                        console.error('❌ Error loading corporate content:', error);\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    console.log('🌐 Public network detected - skipping corporate content');\n                }\n            }, 2000); // Wait 2 seconds for network detection to complete\n        } else {\n            console.log('🔐 Page does not need corporate content');\n        }"

Excellent! The push was successful. Now let me provide a summary of the fix:

## ✅ Fixed: Corporate Content Loading Issue

I've successfully fixed the issue where corporate content was being displayed even when users were on public networks. Here's what was wrong and how I fixed it:

### The Problem
The corporate content loader was auto-loading corporate content without checking if the network detection had authorized access. This caused BMW-specific content to appear even when the network detection correctly identified that the user was on a public network.

### The Solution
1. **Network Detection Integration**: Modified the corporate content loader to check the global `isCorporateNetworkDetected` variable set by the network detection script
2. **Timing Coordination**: Added a 2-second delay to allow network detection to complete before checking authorization
3. **Authorization Check**: Corporate content now only loads when network detection confirms BMW corporate network access

### Key Changes Made
- **`corporate-content-loader.js`**: Updated the auto-loading logic to respect network detection results
- **Cache buster**: Updated timestamp to `2025-09-21T08:45:00Z` to force browser refresh
- **`main.html`**: Updated cache buster in template

### How It Works Now
1. Page loads and both scripts initialize
2. Network detection runs and determines if user is on BMW corporate network
3. Corporate content loader waits 2 seconds for network detection to complete
4. If authorized (corporate network), loads and displays corporate content
5. If not authorized (public network), skips corporate content loading

The fix has been committed and pushed to GitHub. The GitHub Pages deployment will automatically update the published site with this fix, ensuring that corporate content only appears for users actually on the BMW corporate network.

      ```javascript
      // Auto-load corporate content when needed and authorized
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
          console.log('🔐 Corporate content loader initialized');
          
          // Check if current page needs corporate content
          if (window.CorporateContentLoader.isCorporateContentNeeded()) {
              console.log('🔐 Page needs corporate content, checking network authorization...');
              
              // Wait a bit for network detection to complete
              setTimeout(async () => {
                  // Check if network detection has authorized corporate content access
                  // This checks the global variable set by network-detection.js
                  const isAuthorized = window.isCorporateNetworkDetected || 
                                     (typeof isCorporateNetworkDetected !== 'undefined' && isCorporateNetworkDetected);
                  
                  if (isAuthorized) {
                      console.log('✅ Corporate network detected - loading corporate content');
                      try {
                          const loaded = await window.CorporateContentLoader.load();
                          if (loaded) {
                              console.log('✅ Corporate content loaded successfully');
                          } else {
                              console.log('❌ Corporate content loading failed or content not available');
                          }
                      } catch (error) {
                          console.error('❌ Error loading corporate content:', error);
                      }
                  } else {
                      console.log('🌐 Public network detected - skipping corporate content');
                  }
              }, 2000); // Wait 2 seconds for network detection to complete
          } else {
              console.log('🔐 Page does not need corporate content');
          }
      });
      ```

     1→/**
     2→ * Network Detection and Conditional Content Display
     3→ * Shows BMW-specific content only when accessed from corporate network
     4→ * Updated: Removed all manual corporate mode switching capabilities
     5→ */
     6→
     7→(function() {
     8→    'use strict';
     9→    
    10→    // CONFIGURATION: Define which pages get corporate content treatment
    11→    const CORPORATE_CONTENT_PAGES = {
    12→        // Session 10 page
    13→        '/03_mcp-acp-a2a/Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment/': {
    14→            enabled: true,
    15→            hashTriggers: ['session10-corporate-only', 'session10-corporate-content'],
    16→            contentFile: '03_mcp-acp-a2a/Session10_Enterprise_Integration_Production_Deployment.md'
    17→        },
    18→        // Coder setup page  
    19→        '/00_intro/coder/': {
    20→            enabled: true,
    21→            hashTriggers: [],
    22→            contentFile: '00_intro/coder-detailed.md'
    23→        }
    24→    };
    25→    
    26→    // Check if current page is configured for corporate content
    27→    function isPageConfiguredForCorporateContent() {
    28→        const currentPath = window.location.pathname;
    29→        const currentHash = window.location.hash;
    30→        
    31→        for (const [path, config] of Object.entries(CORPORATE_CONTENT_PAGES)) {
    32→            if (!config.enabled) continue;
    33→            
    34→            // Check if current path matches
    35→            if (currentPath.includes(path)) {
    36→                return true;
    37→            }
    38→            
    39→            // Check if hash triggers match
    40→            if (config.hashTriggers && config.hashTriggers.length > 0) {
    41→                for (const trigger of config.hashTriggers) {
    42→                    if (currentHash.includes(trigger)) {
    43→                        return true;
    44→                    }
    45→                }
    46→            }
    47→        }
    48→        
    49→        return false;
    50→    }
    51→    
    52→    // Early exit if not on a corporate content page - ZERO interference
    53→    if (!isPageConfiguredForCorporateContent()) {
    54→        console.log('✅ Regular page detected - corporate content system disabled');
    55→        return; // Exit completely - no event listeners, no functions, nothing
    56→    }
    57→    
    58→    console.log('🏢 Corporate content page detected - initializing enhanced navigation');
    59→    
    60→    // Global variable to track corporate network status
    61→    let isCorporateNetworkDetected = false;
    62→    
    63→    // Debounce mechanism to prevent multiple simultaneous detection cycles
    64→    let detectionInProgress = false;
    65→    let detectionTimeout = null;
    66→
    67→    // BMW corporate network detection
    68→    function isCorporateNetwork() {
    69→        // Check if accessing from BMW corporate network indicators
    70→        const hostname = window.location.hostname;
    71→        const host = window.location.host;
    72→        
    73→        // Corporate network indicators
    74→        const corporateIndicators = [
    75→            // Internal IP ranges (adjust as needed)
    76→            /^10\./,
    77→            /^192\.168\./,
    78→            /^172\.(1[6-9]|2[0-9]|3[01])\./,
    79→            // BMW-specific domains
    80→            /bmw\.com$/,
    81→            /bmwgroup\.com$/
    82→        ];
    83→
    84→        // Check hostname against corporate patterns
    85→        for (const pattern of corporateIndicators) {
    86→            if (pattern.test(hostname) || pattern.test(host)) {
    87→                console.log('Corporate network detected via hostname:', hostname);
    88→                return true;
    89→            }
    90→        }
    91→
    92→        // For development/testing - check if we're on GitHub Pages from public internet
    93→        if (hostname.includes('github.io')) {
    94→            console.log('GitHub Pages detected - showing public content');
    95→            return false;
    96→        }
    97→
    98→        // For localhost/127.0.0.1 - let the CN detection determine access
    99→        if (hostname === 'localhost' || hostname === '127.0.0.1') {
   100→            console.log('Localhost detected - running CN detection to determine access');
   101→            return false; // Let checkInternalService() determine corporate access
   102→        }
   103→
   104→        // Check user agent or other indicators that might suggest corporate network
   105→        // This is a fallback check
   106→        console.log('No corporate network indicators found for hostname:', hostname);
   107→
   108→        // Default to public network if no corporate indicators found
   109→        return false;
   110→    }
   111→
   112→    function checkInternalService() {
   113→        // Run internal service check to detect corporate network access
   114→        console.log('Running internal service check to detect corporate network access');
   115→        
   116→        // Show initial status
   117→        updateNetworkStatusIndicator('checking');
   118→        
   119→        // Try multiple detection methods
   120→        let detectionComplete = false;
   121→        
   122→        // Method 1: URL parameter override REMOVED to prevent manual corporate mode switching
   123→        
   124→        // Method 2: Check external IP first, then try internal service
   125→        console.log('🔍 Checking BMW network access');
   126→        console.log('🌍 Current hostname:', window.location.hostname);
   127→        console.log('🌍 Current URL:', window.location.href);
   128→        
   129→        // Check external IP for BMW ranges (this was working before!)
   130→        fetch('https://api.ipify.org?format=json')
   131→            .then(response => response.json())
   132→            .then(data => {
   133→                console.log('🌐 External IP detected:', data.ip);
   134→                // BMW corporate IP ranges
   135→                const corporateIPPatterns = [
   136→                    /^160\.46\./,    // Your working IP range
   137→                    /^194\.114\./,   // BMW public IP range
   138→                    /^195\.34\./,    // BMW public IP range
   139→                    /^212\.204\./    // BMW public IP range
   140→                ];
   141→                
   142→                const isCorporateIP = corporateIPPatterns.some(pattern => {
   143→                    if (pattern.test(data.ip)) {
   144→                        console.log(`✅ IP ${data.ip} matches corporate pattern: ${pattern}`);
   145→                        return true;
   146→                    }
   147→                    return false;
   148→                });
   149→                
   150→                if (isCorporateIP && !detectionComplete) {
   151→                    console.log('✅ Corporate IP range detected - showing corporate content');
   152→                    detectionComplete = true;
   153→                    showCorporateContent();
   154→                } else if (!detectionComplete) {
   155→                    console.log(`📍 IP ${data.ip} not in corporate ranges, trying internal service check`);
   156→                    tryInternalServiceCheck();
   157→                }
   158→            })
   159→            .catch(error => {
   160→                console.log('❌ IP detection failed, trying internal service check:', error);
   161→                tryInternalServiceCheck();
   162→            });
   163→            
   164→        function tryInternalServiceCheck() {
   165→            if (detectionComplete) return;
   166→            
   167→            // Try internal service check with BMW Content Hub only (no 10.x latency)
   168→            const testUrls = [
   169→                'https://contenthub.bmwgroup.net/favicon.ico'  // BMW Content Hub (most reliable, no VPN latency)
   170→            ];
   171→            
   172→            let urlIndex = 0;
   173→            
   174→            function testNextUrl() {
   175→                if (urlIndex >= testUrls.length || detectionComplete) {
   176→                    // All URLs failed
   177→                    if (!detectionComplete) {
   178→                        console.log('❌ All internal service checks failed - showing public content');
   179→                        hideCorporateContent();
   180→                        detectionComplete = true;
   181→                    }
   182→                    return;
   183→                }
   184→                
   185→                const testUrl = testUrls[urlIndex];
   186→                console.log(`🔍 Trying internal service: ${testUrl}`);
   187→                
   188→                const img = new Image();
   189→                img.onload = function() {
   190→                    if (!detectionComplete) {
   191→                        console.log('✅ Internal service reachable - showing corporate content');
   192→                        showCorporateContent();
   193→                        detectionComplete = true;
   194→                    }
   195→                };
   196→                img.onerror = function() {
   197→                    console.log(`❌ Failed to reach: ${testUrl}`);
   198→                    urlIndex++;
   199→                    setTimeout(testNextUrl, 500); // Try next URL after short delay
   200→                };
   201→                
   202→                img.src = testUrl + '?' + Date.now();
   203→            }
   204→            
   205→            testNextUrl();
   206→        }
   207→        
   208→        // Set a timeout to ensure we don't wait forever  
   209→        setTimeout(() => {
   210→            if (!detectionComplete) {
   211→                console.log('⏱️ BMW ContentHub check timed out after 2s - defaulting to public content');
   212→                hideCorporateContent();
   213→                detectionComplete = true;
   214→            }
   215→        }, 2000);
   216→    }
   217→
   218→    async function showCorporateContent() {
   219→        // Corporate content is only shown when CN detection succeeds
   220→        // No hostname restrictions - let the CN detection determine access
   221→        
   222→        console.log('🏢 Showing BMW corporate content');
   223→        
   224→        // Set global flag to prevent MutationObserver from re-hiding content
   225→        isCorporateNetworkDetected = true;
   226→        
   227→        const corporateElements = document.querySelectorAll('.bmw-corporate-only');
   228→        console.log(`Found ${corporateElements.length} corporate elements to show`);
   229→        corporateElements.forEach((element) => {
   230→            element.classList.add('show-corporate');
   231→            element.classList.add('corporate-network-detected');
   232→        });
   233→
   234→        const publicElements = document.querySelectorAll('.bmw-public-alternative');
   235→        console.log(`Found ${publicElements.length} public elements to hide`);
   236→        publicElements.forEach((element) => {
   237→            element.classList.add('hide-public');
   238→        });
   239→
   240→        // Hide public navigation items and show corporate ones
   241→        hidePublicNavigationItems();
   242→        showCorporateNavigationItems();
   243→
   244→        console.log('🏢 Corporate mode: BMW content enabled');
   245→        
   246→        // Load encrypted corporate content if available and needed
   247→        if (window.CorporateContentLoader) {
   248→            try {
   249→                const loaded = await window.CorporateContentLoader.load();
   250→                if (loaded) {
   251→                    console.log('✅ Corporate content decrypted and loaded');
   252→                }
   253→            } catch (error) {
   254→                console.warn('⚠️ Corporate content not available:', error.message);
   255→            }
   256→        }
   257→
   258→        // Update any dynamic text content
   259→        updateNetworkSpecificContent(true);
   260→        
   261→        // Update network status indicator
   262→        updateNetworkStatusIndicator('corporate');
   263→    }
   264→
   265→    function hideCorporateContent() {
   266→        console.log('🌐 Showing public content');
   267→        
   268→        // Clear global flag to allow MutationObserver to hide BMW content
   269→        isCorporateNetworkDetected = false;
   270→        
   271→        const corporateElements = document.querySelectorAll('.bmw-corporate-only');
   272→        console.log(`Found ${corporateElements.length} corporate elements to hide`);
   273→        corporateElements.forEach(element => {
   274→            element.classList.remove('show-corporate');
   275→            element.classList.remove('corporate-network-detected');
   276→        });
   277→
   278→        const publicElements = document.querySelectorAll('.bmw-public-alternative');
   279→        console.log(`Found ${publicElements.length} public elements to show`);
   280→        publicElements.forEach(element => {
   281→            element.classList.remove('hide-public');
   282→            element.classList.add('public-network-detected');
   283→        });
   284→
   285→        // Hide corporate navigation items and show public ones  
   286→        hideCorporateNavigationItems();
   287→        showPublicNavigationItems();
   288→        removeSession10Navigation();
   289→
   290→        console.log('📋 Public mode: public content visible');
   291→        
   292→
   293→        // Update any dynamic text content
   294→        updateNetworkSpecificContent(false);
   295→        
   296→        // Update network status indicator
   297→        updateNetworkStatusIndicator('public');
   298→    }

   311→                        <li>Use your BMW credentials to log in</li>
   312→                        <li>Launch your pre-configured environment</li>
   313→                    </ol>
   314→                `;
   315→            } else {
   316→                setupInstructions.innerHTML = `
   317→                    <h3>🌐 Public Network - Local Setup Required</h3>
   318→                    <p><strong>Set up your local development environment:</strong></p>
   319→                    <ol>
   320→                        <li>Install Python 3.11+</li>
   321→                        <li>Clone the repository</li>
   322→                        <li>Install dependencies per module requirements</li>
   323→                        <li>Configure your own LLM API keys</li>
   324→                    </ol>
   325→                `;
   326→            }
   327→        }
   328→    }

   330→    function updateNetworkStatusIndicator(networkType) {
   331→        // Only show indicator on Setup & Environment pages
   332→        const currentPath = window.location.pathname;
   333→        const isSetupPage = currentPath.includes('00_intro') || 
   334→                           currentPath.includes('setup') || 
   335→                           currentPath.includes('environment') ||
   336→                           currentPath.includes('coder') ||
   337→                           currentPath.includes('llmapi');
   338→        
   339→        // Remove any existing status indicator
   340→        const existingIndicator = document.querySelector('.network-status-indicator');
   341→        if (existingIndicator) {
   342→            existingIndicator.remove();
   343→        }
   344→
   345→        // Don't show indicator if not on setup pages
   346→        if (!isSetupPage) {
   347→            return;
   348→        }
   349→
   350→        // Create new status indicator
   351→        const indicator = document.createElement('div');
   352→        indicator.className = 'network-status-indicator';
   353→        indicator.style.cssText = `
   354→            position: fixed;
   355→            bottom: 20px;
   356→            right: 20px;
   357→            background: ${networkType === 'corporate' ? '#0066cc' : '#28a745'};
   358→            color: white;
   359→            padding: 8px 12px;
   360→            border-radius: 4px;
   361→            font-size: 12px;
   362→            font-weight: bold;
   363→            z-index: 1000;
   364→            box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
   365→            font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Segoe UI", Roboto, sans-serif;
   366→        `;
   367→        
   368→        if (networkType === 'corporate') {
   369→            indicator.innerHTML = `
   370→                🏢 BMW Corporate Network
   371→                <div style="font-size: 10px; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 2px;">
   372→                    Cloud Dev Environment Available
   373→                </div>
   374→            `;
   375→        } else if (networkType === 'checking') {
   376→            indicator.innerHTML = `
   377→                🔍 Detecting Network...
   378→                <div style="font-size: 10px; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 2px;">
   379→                    Checking corporate access
   380→                </div>
   381→            `;
   382→            indicator.style.background = '#ffa500';
   383→        } else {
   384→            indicator.innerHTML = `
   385→                🌐 Public Network
   386→                <div style="font-size: 10px; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 2px;">
   387→                    Local Setup Required
   388→                </div>
   389→            `;
   390→        }
   391→
   392→        // Remove manual override clickability to prevent switching to corporate network
   393→        // This was causing unwanted CN switching when viewing publicly
   394→        indicator.style.cursor = 'default';
   395→        indicator.title = networkType === 'corporate' ? 
   396→            'BMW Corporate Network - Cloud Development Environment Available' : 
   397→            'Public Network - Local Setup Required';
   398→
   399→        document.body.appendChild(indicator);
   400→
   401→        // Auto-hide after 5 seconds
   402→        setTimeout(() => {
   403→            if (indicator && indicator.parentNode) {
   404→                indicator.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease';
   405→                indicator.style.opacity = '0';
   406→                setTimeout(() => {
   407→                    if (indicator && indicator.parentNode) {
   408→                        indicator.remove();
   409→                    }
   410→                }, 500);
   411→            }
   412→        }, 5000);
   413→    }
   414→
   415→    function initializeNetworkDetection() {
   416→        // Add CSS for smooth transitions and ensure BMW content is hidden by default on public sites
   417→        const style = document.createElement('style');
   418→        const hostname = window.location.hostname;
   419→        const isPublicSite = hostname.includes('github.io') || hostname.includes('fwornle');
   420→        
   421→        style.textContent = `
   422→            /* Default: hide all conditional content until detection completes */
   423→            .bmw-corporate-only {
   424→                display: none;
   425→                transition: opacity 0.3s ease-in-out;
   426→            }
   427→            .bmw-public-alternative {
   428→                display: none;
   429→                transition: opacity 0.3s ease-in-out;
   430→            }
   431→            /* Show corporate content when detected */
   432→            .bmw-corporate-only.corporate-network-detected {
   433→                display: block;
   434→                animation: fadeIn 0.5s ease-in-out;
   435→            }
   436→            /* Show public content when detected */
   437→            .bmw-public-alternative.public-network-detected {
   438→                display: block;
   439→                animation: fadeIn 0.5s ease-in-out;
   440→            }
   441→            @keyframes fadeIn {
   442→                from { opacity: 0; }
   443→                to { opacity: 1; }
   444→            }
   445→            /* Ensure setup instructions container is visible */
   446→            .setup-instructions {
   447→                min-height: 100px;
   448→            }
   449→        `;
   450→        document.head.appendChild(style);
   451→
   452→        // Always run CN detection regardless of hostname
   453→        console.log('Running corporate network detection...');
   454→        
   455→        // Initial quick check, then run full detection
   456→        if (isCorporateNetwork()) {
   457→            console.log('Corporate network detected initially');
   458→            showCorporateContent();
   459→        } else {
   460→            console.log('Public network assumed initially, running full CN detection');
   461→            hideCorporateContent();
   462→            // Always run the comprehensive check for CN access
   463→            checkInternalService();
   464→        }
   465→    }
   466→
   467→    function cleanupNavigationState() {
   468→        // Clean up any previous navigation state
   469→        // We're on a corporate page, so just reset for fresh setup
   470→        if (window.corporateScrollListener) {
   471→            window.removeEventListener('scroll', window.corporateScrollListener);
   472→            window.corporateScrollListener = null;
   473→            console.log('🧹 Cleaned up previous corporate scroll listener');
   474→        }
   475→    }
   476→
   477→    // Initialize when DOM is ready and on every page load
   478→    function runDetection() {
   479→        // Prevent multiple simultaneous detections
   480→        if (detectionInProgress) {
   481→            console.log('🔄 Detection already in progress, skipping...');
   482→            return;
   483→        }
   484→        
   485→        // Clear any pending detection
   486→        if (detectionTimeout) {
   487→            clearTimeout(detectionTimeout);
   488→        }
   489→        
   490→        // Debounce detection to prevent rapid successive calls
   491→        detectionTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
   492→            if (detectionInProgress) return;
   493→            
   494→            detectionInProgress = true;
   495→            console.log('🔄 Starting fresh network detection...');
   496→            
   497→            // Clean up navigation state first
   498→            cleanupNavigationState();
   499→            
   500→            try {
   501→                initializeNetworkDetection();
   502→            } finally {
   503→                // Reset detection flag after a delay to allow for async operations
   504→                setTimeout(() => {
   505→                    detectionInProgress = false;
   506→                }, 2000);
   507→            }
   508→        }, 100);
   509→    }
   510→    
   511→    // Initial run
   512→    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
   513→        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', runDetection);
   514→    } else {
   515→        runDetection();
   516→    }
   517→    
   518→    // Set up navigation listeners immediately (not waiting for DOMContentLoaded)
   519→    console.log('🎯 Setting up navigation listeners');
   520→    
   521→    // Watch for URL changes with MutationObserver
   522→    let lastUrl = location.href;
   523→    const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
   524→        const url = location.href;
   525→        if (url !== lastUrl) {
   526→            lastUrl = url;
   527→            console.log('📍 URL changed to:', url);
   528→            
   529→            // Reset Session 10 loaded flag when navigating to different pages
   530→            if (!url.includes('session10-corporate') && !url.includes('Session10_Enterprise_Integration')) {
   531→                session10Loaded = false;
   532→            }
   533→            
   534→            // No cleanup needed - if we navigate away, the page will reload
   535→            // and our early exit will prevent this code from running
   536→            
   537→            setTimeout(runDetection, 100);
   538→        }
   539→    });
   540→    observer.observe(document.body || document.documentElement, {
   541→        subtree: true, 
   542→        childList: true
   543→    });
   544→    
   545→    // Listen for navigation link clicks (use capturing to catch all clicks)
   546→    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   547→        const link = e.target.closest('a');
   548→        if (link) {
   549→            const href = link.getAttribute('href');
   550→            console.log('🔗 Link clicked:', href);
   551→            if (link.classList.contains('md-nav__link') || 
   552→                link.classList.contains('md-tabs__link') ||
   553→                href?.includes('/00_intro/')) {
   554→                console.log('🔗 Navigation link detected, will re-run detection');
   555→                setTimeout(runDetection, 500);
   556→            }
   557→        }
   558→    }, true); // Use capture phase
   559→    
   560→    // Also listen for popstate
   561→    window.addEventListener('popstate', () => {
   562→        console.log('⬅️ Browser navigation detected');
   563→        
   564→        // Reset Session 10 loaded flag when navigating back/forward
   565→        const url = location.href;
   566→        if (!url.includes('session10-corporate') && !url.includes('Session10_Enterprise_Integration')) {
   567→            session10Loaded = false;
   568→        }
   569→        
   570→        runDetection();
   571→    });
   572→
   573→    // Navigation control functions
   574→    function hideCorporateNavigationItems() {
   575→        const navigationItems = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
   576→        navigationItems.forEach(link => {
   577→            const linkText = link.textContent.trim();
   578→            // Hide items that contain corporate/BMW content indicators
   579→            if (linkText.includes('BMW Gaia LLM API') || 
   580→                linkText.includes('BMW Cloud Development Environment with Coder') ||
   581→                linkText.includes('Quick Setup') ||
   582→                linkText.includes('Testing Your Connection') ||
   583→                linkText.includes('Available Models') ||
   584→                linkText.includes('Using in Code') ||
   585→                linkText.includes('Framework Integration') ||
   586→                linkText.includes('Why Cloud Development?') ||
   587→                linkText.includes('AI Assistant Integration')) {
   588→                const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   589→                if (listItem) {
   590→                    console.log('Hiding corporate nav item:', linkText);
   591→                    listItem.style.display = 'none';
   592→                }
   593→            }
   594→        });
   595→    }
   596→
   597→    function showCorporateNavigationItems() {
   598→        const navigationItems = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
   599→        navigationItems.forEach(link => {
   600→            const linkText = link.textContent.trim();
   601→            // Show items that contain corporate/BMW content indicators
   602→            if (linkText.includes('BMW Gaia LLM API') || 
   603→                linkText.includes('BMW Cloud Development Environment with Coder') ||
   604→                linkText.includes('Quick Setup') ||
   605→                linkText.includes('Testing Your Connection') ||
   606→                linkText.includes('Available Models') ||
   607→                linkText.includes('Using in Code') ||
   608→                linkText.includes('Framework Integration') ||
   609→                linkText.includes('Why Cloud Development?') ||
   610→                linkText.includes('AI Assistant Integration')) {
   611→                const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   612→                if (listItem) {
   613→                    console.log('Showing corporate nav item:', linkText);
   614→                    listItem.style.display = '';
   615→                }
   616→            }
   617→        });
   618→        
   619→        // Add Session 10 to Module 03 navigation when in corporate mode
   620→        addSession10Navigation();
   621→    }
   622→
   623→    function addSession10Navigation() {
   624→        // Find Session 9 in Module 03 navigation and add Session 10 after it
   625→        const session9Link = document.querySelector('a[href*="Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment"]');
   626→        if (session9Link) {
   627→            const session9Item = session9Link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   628→            if (session9Item && !document.querySelector('.bmw-corporate-nav-item')) {
   629→                console.log('🔧 Adding Session 10 to corporate navigation');
   630→                
   631→                // Create Session 10 navigation item
   632→                const session10Item = document.createElement('li');
   633→                session10Item.className = 'md-nav__item bmw-corporate-nav-item';
   634→                
   635→                const session10Link = document.createElement('a');
   636→                session10Link.href = '#session10-corporate-only';
   637→                session10Link.className = 'md-nav__link bmw-corporate-link';
   638→                session10Link.textContent = 'Session 10 - Enterprise Integration';
   639→                
   640→                // Add click handler to load corporate content
   641→                session10Link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   642→                    e.preventDefault();
   643→                    loadCorporateSession10();
   644→                });
   645→                
   646→                session10Item.appendChild(session10Link);
   647→                
   648→                // Insert after Session 9
   649→                session9Item.parentNode.insertBefore(session10Item, session9Item.nextSibling);
   650→                
   651→                console.log('✅ Session 10 added to corporate navigation');
   652→            }
   653→        }
   654→        
   655→        // Also update the "Next" link on Session 9 to point to Session 10
   656→        updateSession9NextLink();
   657→    }
   658→
   659→    function updateSession9NextLink() {
   660→        // Find "Next" navigation links and update Session 9 to point to Session 10
   661→        const nextLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.md-footer__link--next');
   662→        nextLinks.forEach(link => {
   663→            if (window.location.pathname.includes('Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment')) {
   664→                const titleDiv = link.querySelector('.md-ellipsis');
   665→                if (titleDiv) {
   666→                    titleDiv.textContent = 'Session 10 - Enterprise Integration';
   667→                    link.href = '#session10-corporate-only';
   668→                    
   669→                    // Add click handler for corporate Session 10
   670→                    link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   671→                        e.preventDefault();
   672→                        loadCorporateSession10();
   673→                    });
   674→                    
   675→                    console.log('🔧 Updated Session 9 next link to point to Session 10');
   676→                }
   677→            }
   678→        });
   679→    }
   680→
   681→    // Track if Session 10 content is currently loaded to prevent multiple loads
   682→    let session10Loaded = false;
   683→    
   684→    window.loadCorporateSession10 = async function() {
   685→        console.log('🔐 Loading corporate Session 10 content...');
   686→        
   687→        // Prevent multiple loads of Session 10 content
   688→        if (session10Loaded) {
   689→            console.log('📄 Session 10 already loaded, skipping...');
   690→            return true;
   691→        }
   692→        
   693→        // Retry mechanism for improved reliability
   694→        const maxRetries = 3;
   695→        let retryCount = 0;
   696→        
   697→        while (retryCount < maxRetries) {
   698→            try {
   699→                console.log(`🔄 Attempt ${retryCount + 1}/${maxRetries} to load Session 10...`);
   700→                
   701→                // Check if corporate content loader exists
   702→                if (!window.CorporateContentLoader) {
   703→                    console.warn('⚠️ Corporate content loader not available, waiting...');
   704→                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
   705→                    retryCount++;
   706→                    continue;
   707→                }
   708→                
   709→                // If content is not loaded yet, try to load it first
   710→                if (!window.CorporateContentLoader.loadedContent) {
   711→                    console.log('📥 Corporate content not loaded yet, loading now...');
   712→                    const loaded = await window.CorporateContentLoader.load();
   713→                    if (!loaded) {
   714→                        console.warn('⚠️ Failed to load corporate content, retrying...');
   715→                        retryCount++;
   716→                        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
   717→                        continue;
   718→                    }
   719→                    console.log('✅ Corporate content loaded successfully');
   720→                }
   721→                
   722→                // Now check for Session 10 content
   723→                const session10Content = window.CorporateContentLoader.loadedContent['03_mcp-acp-a2a/Session10_Enterprise_Integration_Production_Deployment.md'];
   724→                if (session10Content) {
   725→                    console.log('📄 Found Session 10 content, replacing page...');
   726→                    session10Loaded = true;
   727→                    
   728→                    // Update page title
   729→                    document.title = 'Session 10: Enterprise Integration & Production Deployment | Agentic AI Nano-Degree';
   730→                    
   731→                    // Update URL without causing page reload - use hash instead of path to avoid 404s
   732→                    if (history.pushState) {
   733→                        // Use hash-based navigation to avoid creating non-existent paths
   734→                        const baseUrl = window.location.pathname.replace(/#.*$/, '');
   735→                        const newUrl = baseUrl + '#session10-corporate-content';
   736→                        history.pushState({page: 'session10'}, '', newUrl);
   737→                    }
   738→                    
   739→                    // Replace page content
   740→                    await window.CorporateContentLoader.replacePageContent(session10Content);
   741→                    
   742→                    // Wait a bit for content to be injected, then update navigation
   743→                    setTimeout(async () => {
   744→                        await updateMkDocsNavigationForCorporateContent(session10Content);
   745→                    }, 100);
   746→                    
   747→                    // Instantly jump to top of the page after content is loaded
   748→                    setTimeout(() => {
   749→                        window.scrollTo(0, 0);
   750→                        console.log('📍 Jumped to top of Session 10 content');
   751→                    }, 200);
   752→                    
   753→                    console.log('✅ Session 10 corporate content loaded successfully');
   754→                    return true;
   755→                    
   756→                } else {
   757→                    console.warn('⚠️ Session 10 content not found in encrypted data, retrying...');
   758→                    console.log('Available content keys:', Object.keys(window.CorporateContentLoader.loadedContent || {}));
   759→                    retryCount++;
   760→                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
   761→                    continue;
   762→                }
   763→                
   764→            } catch (error) {
   765→                console.warn(`⚠️ Error loading Session 10 (attempt ${retryCount + 1}):`, error);
   766→                retryCount++;
   767→                if (retryCount < maxRetries) {
   768→                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
   769→                }
   770→            }
   771→        }
   772→        
   773→        console.error('❌ Failed to load Session 10 after all retries');
   774→        return false;
   775→    }
   776→
   777→    async function updateMkDocsNavigationForCorporateContent(contentMarkdown) {
   778→        console.log('🔧 Updating MkDocs navigation for corporate content...');
   779→        
   780→        // No guard needed - we're already on a corporate content page if this runs
   781→        
   782→        try {
   783→            // Extract metadata from the content itself
   784→            const contentMetadata = extractContentMetadata(contentMarkdown);
   785→            console.log('📄 Detected content metadata:', contentMetadata);
   786→            
   787→            // Wait for MkDocs navigation to be ready (retry mechanism)
   788→            let attempts = 0;
   789→            const maxAttempts = 5;
   790→            let corporateNavItem = null;
   791→            
   792→            while (!corporateNavItem && attempts < maxAttempts) {
   793→                if (attempts > 0) {
   794→                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 200 * attempts)); // Progressive delay
   795→                }
   796→                
   797→                // Debug: List all navigation links on first attempt
   798→                if (attempts === 0) {
   799→                    const allNavLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
   800→                    console.log('🔍 Debug - All navigation links found:', allNavLinks.length);
   801→                    console.log('🔍 Navigation structure:', Array.from(allNavLinks).slice(0, 10).map(link => ({
   802→                        href: link.getAttribute('href'),
   803→                        text: link.textContent.trim(),
   804→                        active: link.classList.contains('md-nav__link--active')
   805→                    })));
   806→                }
   807→                
   808→                // First try to find current active navigation item
   809→                corporateNavItem = document.querySelector('.md-nav__link--active')?.closest('.md-nav__item');
   810→                
   811→                if (!corporateNavItem) {
   812→                    // Try specific Session 9 patterns
   813→                    const session9Selectors = [
   814→                        'a[href*="Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment"]',
   815→                        'a[href*="Session9"]',
   816→                        'a[href*="Production_Agent_Deployment"]'
   817→                    ];
   818→                    
   819→                    for (const selector of session9Selectors) {
   820→                        corporateNavItem = document.querySelector(selector)?.closest('.md-nav__item');
   821→                        if (corporateNavItem) {
   822→                            console.log(`🎯 Found via selector: ${selector}`);
   823→                            break;
   824→                        }
   825→                    }
   826→                }
   827→                
   828→                if (!corporateNavItem) {
   829→                    // Fallback: try any MCP/ACP section navigation item
   830→                    corporateNavItem = document.querySelector([
   831→                        'a[href*="03_mcp-acp-a2a"]',
   832→                        'a[href*="mcp-acp-a2a"]'
   833→                    ].join(', '))?.closest('.md-nav__item');
   834→                }
   835→                
   836→                attempts++;
   837→                console.log(`🔍 Navigation search attempt ${attempts}/${maxAttempts}, found:`, !!corporateNavItem);
   838→                
   839→                if (corporateNavItem) {
   840→                    const navLink = corporateNavItem.querySelector('.md-nav__link');
   841→                    console.log('🔍 Found navigation item:', {
   842→                        href: navLink?.getAttribute('href'),
   843→                        text: navLink?.textContent?.trim(),
   844→                        outerHTML: corporateNavItem.outerHTML.substring(0, 200) + '...'
   845→                    });
   846→                }
   847→            }
   848→            
   849→            if (corporateNavItem) {
   850→                // Remove active state from all navigation items
   851→                document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__item').forEach(item => {
   852→                    item.classList.remove('md-nav__item--active');
   853→                    const link = item.querySelector('.md-nav__link');
   854→                    if (link) {
   855→                        link.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active');
   856→                    }
   857→                });
   858→                
   859→                // Activate corporate content navigation item
   860→                corporateNavItem.classList.add('md-nav__item--active');
   861→                const corporateLink = corporateNavItem.querySelector('.md-nav__link');
   862→                if (corporateLink) {
   863→                    corporateLink.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
   864→                    // Update the link text to match current content
   865→                    if (contentMetadata.title) {
   866→                        corporateLink.textContent = contentMetadata.title;
   867→                    }
   868→                }
   869→                
   870→                // Create corporate content sub-navigation based on content structure
   871→                createCorporateContentSubNavigation(corporateNavItem, contentMetadata);
   872→                
   873→                // Scroll corporate content item into view in sidebar
   874→                corporateNavItem.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
   875→                
   876→                console.log(`✅ MkDocs navigation updated for ${contentMetadata.title || 'corporate content'}`);
   877→            } else {
   878→                console.warn('⚠️ Corporate content navigation item not found');
   879→            }
   880→            
   881→            // Fix potential sidebar styling conflicts
   882→            fixSidebarStylingConflicts();
   883→            
   884→        } catch (error) {
   885→            console.error('❌ Failed to update MkDocs navigation for corporate content:', error);
   886→        }
   887→    }
   888→
   889→    function extractContentMetadata(markdownContent) {
   890→        const metadata = {
   891→            title: null,
   892→            sections: [],
   893→            type: 'corporate-content'
   894→        };
   895→        
   896→        if (!markdownContent) return metadata;
   897→        
   898→        // Extract title from first H1
   899→        const titleMatch = markdownContent.match(/^#\s+(.+)$/m);
   900→        if (titleMatch) {
   901→            metadata.title = titleMatch[1].trim();
   902→        }
   903→        
   904→        // Extract sections from H2 and H3 headings
   905→        const headingMatches = markdownContent.match(/^#{2,3}\s+(.+)$/gm);
   906→        if (headingMatches) {
   907→            metadata.sections = headingMatches.map(heading => {
   908→                const level = (heading.match(/#/g) || []).length;
   909→                const title = heading.replace(/^#+\s+/, '').trim();
   910→                const id = title.toLowerCase()
   911→                    .replace(/[^a-z0-9\s-]/g, '')
   912→                    .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
   913→                    .replace(/-+/g, '-')
   914→                    .replace(/^-|-$/g, '');
   915→                
   916→                return {
   917→                    level,
   918→                    title,
   919→                    id: id || title.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-'),
   920→                    href: `#${id || title.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-')}`
   921→                };
   922→            });
   923→        }
   924→        
   925→        // Detect content type from title or content
   926→        if (metadata.title) {
   927→            if (metadata.title.includes('Session')) {
   928→                metadata.type = 'session';
   929→                // Extract session number if present
   930→                const sessionMatch = metadata.title.match(/Session\s*(\d+)/i);
   931→                if (sessionMatch) {
   932→                    metadata.sessionNumber = parseInt(sessionMatch[1]);
   933→                }
   934→            } else if (metadata.title.includes('Enterprise') || metadata.title.includes('Production')) {
   935→                metadata.type = 'enterprise-content';
   936→            }
   937→        }
   938→        
   939→        return metadata;
   940→    }
   941→
   942→
   943→    function createCorporateContentSubNavigation(navItem, contentMetadata) {
   944→        console.log(`🔧 Creating sub-navigation for ${contentMetadata.title || 'corporate content'}...`);
   945→        
   946→        // Remove any existing sub-navigation to rebuild with current content
   947→        const existingSubNav = navItem.querySelector('.md-nav');
   948→        if (existingSubNav) {
   949→            existingSubNav.remove();
   950→        }
   951→        
   952→        // Debug content metadata
   953→        console.log('🔍 Content metadata for sub-navigation:', contentMetadata);
   954→        console.log('🔍 Available sections:', contentMetadata.sections);
   955→        
   956→        // Only create sub-navigation if we have sections
   957→        if (contentMetadata.sections && contentMetadata.sections.length > 0) {
   958→            // Create sub-navigation structure
   959→            const subNav = document.createElement('nav');
   960→            subNav.className = 'md-nav md-nav--secondary';
   961→            subNav.setAttribute('aria-label', `${contentMetadata.title || 'Corporate Content'} Navigation`);
   962→            
   963→            const subNavList = document.createElement('ul');
   964→            subNavList.className = 'md-nav__list';
   965→            
   966→            // Create navigation items from content sections
   967→            contentMetadata.sections.forEach(section => {
   968→                const listItem = document.createElement('li');
   969→                listItem.className = 'md-nav__item';
   970→                
   971→                const link = document.createElement('a');
   972→                link.href = section.href;
   973→                link.className = 'md-nav__link';
   974→                link.textContent = section.title;
   975→                
   976→                // Add appropriate nesting class for H3 items
   977→                if (section.level === 3) {
   978→                    listItem.classList.add('md-nav__item--nested');
   979→                }
   980→                
   981→                // Add smooth scroll behavior for anchor links
   982→                link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   983→                    e.preventDefault();
   984→                    const targetId = section.id;
   985→                    const targetElement = document.getElementById(targetId) || 
   986→                                         document.querySelector(`h${section.level}[id="${targetId}"]`) ||
   987→                                         findHeadingByText(section.title);
   988→                    
   989→                    if (targetElement) {
   990→                        targetElement.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
   991→                        // Update URL hash
   992→                        history.pushState(null, '', section.href);
   993→                        
   994→                        // Update active state in sub-navigation
   995→                        subNavList.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link').forEach(l => l.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active'));
   996→                        link.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
   997→                    }
   998→                });
   999→                
  1000→                listItem.appendChild(link);
  1001→                subNavList.appendChild(listItem);
  1002→            });
  1003→            
  1004→            subNav.appendChild(subNavList);
  1005→            navItem.appendChild(subNav);
  1006→            
  1007→            console.log(`✅ Sub-navigation created with ${contentMetadata.sections.length} sections`);
  1008→            
  1009→            // Set up scroll spy for corporate content - we're already on a corporate page
  1010→            setupCorporateContentScrollSpy(subNavList, contentMetadata.sections);
  1011→        }
  1012→        
  1013→        // Mark as corporate content for scroll spy detection
  1014→        document.body.classList.add('corporate-content-active');
  1015→        console.log('🔧 Marked page as corporate content');
  1016→        
  1017→        // Expand the navigation and ensure visibility
  1018→        navItem.classList.add('md-nav__item--nested', 'md-nav__item--active', 'corporate-nav-item');
  1019→        
  1020→        // Make sure the navigation item is visible and expanded
  1021→        const navInput = navItem.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
  1022→        if (navInput) {
  1023→            navInput.checked = true;
  1024→        }
  1025→        
  1026→        // Add explicit CSS to ensure visibility and prevent removal
  1027→        navItem.style.display = 'block !important';
  1028→        navItem.setAttribute('data-corporate-nav', 'true');
  1029→        const subNav = navItem.querySelector('.md-nav');
  1030→        if (subNav) {
  1031→            subNav.style.display = 'block !important';
  1032→            subNav.style.visibility = 'visible';
  1033→            subNav.setAttribute('data-corporate-subnav', 'true');
  1034→        }
  1035→        
  1036→        // Prevent navigation from being hidden by other scripts
  1037→        const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
  1038→            mutations.forEach((mutation) => {
  1039→                if (mutation.type === 'attributes' && mutation.attributeName === 'style') {
  1040→                    const target = mutation.target;
  1041→                    if (target.hasAttribute('data-corporate-nav') || target.hasAttribute('data-corporate-subnav')) {
  1042→                        if (target.style.display === 'none' || target.style.visibility === 'hidden') {
  1043→                            console.log('🔧 Preventing corporate navigation from being hidden');
  1044→                            target.style.display = 'block';
  1045→                            target.style.visibility = 'visible';
  1046→                        }
  1047→                    }
  1048→                }
  1049→            });
  1050→        });
  1051→        
  1052→        observer.observe(navItem, { attributes: true, subtree: true });
  1053→        if (subNav) {
  1054→            observer.observe(subNav, { attributes: true, subtree: true });
  1055→        }
  1056→        
  1057→        console.log('🔧 Navigation item expanded and protected from hiding');
  1058→    }
  1059→
  1060→    function findHeadingByText(text) {
  1061→        // Helper function to find headings by text content
  1062→        const headings = document.querySelectorAll('h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6');
  1063→        for (const heading of headings) {
  1064→            if (heading.textContent.trim().toLowerCase().includes(text.toLowerCase())) {
  1065→                return heading;
  1066→            }
  1067→        }
  1068→        return null;
  1069→    }
  1070→
  1071→    function setupCorporateContentScrollSpy(navList, sections) {
  1072→        console.log('🔍 Setting up scroll spy for corporate content navigation...');
  1073→        
  1074→        let ticking = false;
  1075→        let lastActiveSection = null;
  1076→        let scrollSpyActive = false;
  1077→        
  1078→        function updateActiveNavigation() {
  1079→            if (!navList || !sections) return;
  1080→            
  1081→            // Find which section is currently visible
  1082→            let activeSection = null;
  1083→            const scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
  1084→            
  1085→            // Check each section to find the currently visible one
  1086→            for (let i = sections.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
  1087→                const section = sections[i];
  1088→                const targetElement = document.getElementById(section.id) || 
  1089→                                   document.querySelector(`h${section.level}[id="${section.id}"]`) ||
  1090→                                   findHeadingByText(section.title);
  1091→                
  1092→                if (targetElement) {
  1093→                    const rect = targetElement.getBoundingClientRect();
  1094→                    const elementTop = rect.top + scrollTop;
  1095→                    
  1096→                    // Consider element active if it's within the viewport or just passed
  1097→                    if (elementTop <= scrollTop + 100) {
  1098→                        activeSection = section;
  1099→                        break;
  1100→                    }
  1101→                }
  1102→            }
  1103→            
  1104→            // Update navigation highlighting if section changed
  1105→            if (activeSection && activeSection.id !== lastActiveSection) {
  1106→                // ONLY remove active state from corporate sub-navigation links, not main nav
  1107→                navList.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link').forEach(link => {
  1108→                    link.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active');
  1109→                });
  1110→                
  1111→                // Add active state to current section's nav link
  1112→                const activeLink = navList.querySelector(`a[href="#${activeSection.id}"]`);
  1113→                if (activeLink) {
  1114→                    activeLink.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
  1115→                    console.log(`🔍 Corporate active section: ${activeSection.title}`);
  1116→                }
  1117→                
  1118→                lastActiveSection = activeSection.id;
  1119→            }
  1120→            
  1121→            ticking = false;
  1122→        }
  1123→        
  1124→        function onScroll() {
  1125→            if (!ticking) {
  1126→                requestAnimationFrame(updateActiveNavigation);
  1127→                ticking = true;
  1128→            }
  1129→        }
  1130→        
  1131→        // Clean up any existing scroll listeners for corporate content
  1132→        if (window.corporateScrollListener) {
  1133→            window.removeEventListener('scroll', window.corporateScrollListener);
  1134→        }
  1135→        
  1136→        // Set up scroll listener for corporate content
  1137→        window.corporateScrollListener = onScroll;
  1138→        window.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, { passive: true });
  1139→        console.log('✅ Corporate scroll listener activated');
  1140→        
  1141→        // Initial check
  1142→        updateActiveNavigation();
  1143→        
  1144→        console.log('✅ Corporate content scroll spy setup complete');
  1145→    }
  1146→
  1147→    function fixSidebarStylingConflicts() {
  1148→        console.log('🔧 Fixing sidebar styling conflicts...');
  1149→        
  1150→        // Ensure sidebar scrolling works properly
  1151→        const sidebar = document.querySelector('.md-sidebar--primary .md-sidebar__scrollwrap');
  1152→        if (sidebar) {
  1153→            sidebar.style.overflowY = 'auto';
  1154→            sidebar.style.height = 'calc(100vh - 2.4rem)';
  1155→        }
  1156→        
  1157→        // Fix potential z-index conflicts
  1158→        const sidebarContainer = document.querySelector('.md-sidebar--primary');
  1159→        if (sidebarContainer) {
  1160→            sidebarContainer.style.zIndex = '3';
  1161→        }
  1162→        
  1163→        // Ensure bottom navigation doesn't overlap
  1164→        const bottomNav = document.querySelector('.md-footer');
  1165→        if (bottomNav) {
  1166→            bottomNav.style.position = 'relative';
  1167→            bottomNav.style.zIndex = '1';
  1168→        }
  1169→        
  1170→        // Fix any content overflow issues
  1171→        const contentArea = document.querySelector('.md-content');
  1172→        if (contentArea) {
  1173→            contentArea.style.overflow = 'visible';
  1174→        }
  1175→        
  1176→        console.log('✅ Sidebar styling conflicts fixed');
  1177→    }
  1178→
  1179→    function hidePublicNavigationItems() {
  1180→        const navigationItems = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
  1181→        navigationItems.forEach(link => {
  1182→            const linkText = link.textContent.trim();
  1183→            // Hide items that contain public/local content indicators (but NOT main nav items)
  1184→            if (linkText.includes('Public LLM API Configuration') || 
  1185→                linkText.includes('Local Development Environment Setup') ||
  1186→                linkText.includes('Local Setup Requirements') ||
  1187→                linkText.includes('Setup Steps') ||
  1188→                linkText.includes('OpenAI Setup') ||
  1189→                linkText.includes('Anthropic Claude Setup') ||
  1190→                linkText.includes('Testing Your Setup') ||
  1191→                linkText.includes('Local LLM Options')) {
  1192→                const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
  1193→                if (listItem) {
  1194→                    console.log('Hiding public nav item:', linkText);
  1195→                    listItem.style.display = 'none';
  1196→                }
  1197→            }
  1198→        });
  1199→    }
  1200→
  1201→    function removeSession10Navigation() {
  1202→        // Remove Session 10 from navigation when in public mode
  1203→        const session10Links = document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="Session10_Enterprise_Integration"]');
  1204→        session10Links.forEach(link => {
  1205→            const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
  1206→            if (listItem && listItem.classList.contains('bmw-corporate-nav-item')) {
  1207→                console.log('🗑️ Removing Session 10 from public navigation');
  1208→                listItem.remove();
  1209→            }
  1210→        });
  1211→        
  1212→        // Reset Session 10 loaded flag when switching to public mode
  1213→        session10Loaded = false;
  1214→        
  1215→        // Update Session 9 next link to not point to Session 10
  1216→        const nextLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.md-footer__link--next');
  1217→        nextLinks.forEach(link => {
  1218→            if (window.location.pathname.includes('Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment')) {
  1219→                // Remove the next link entirely for Session 9 in public mode
  1220→                const titleDiv = link.querySelector('.md-ellipsis');
  1221→                if (titleDiv && titleDiv.textContent.includes('Session 10')) {
  1222→                    console.log('🗑️ Removing Session 9 next link to Session 10 in public mode');
  1223→                    link.style.display = 'none';
  1224→                }
  1225→            }
  1226→        });
  1227→    }
  1228→
  1229→    function showPublicNavigationItems() {
  1230→        const navigationItems = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
  1231→        navigationItems.forEach(link => {
  1232→            const linkText = link.textContent.trim();
  1233→            // Show items that contain public/local content indicators (but NOT main nav items)
  1234→            if (linkText.includes('Public LLM API Configuration') || 
  1235→                linkText.includes('Local Development Environment Setup') ||
  1236→                linkText.includes('Local Setup Requirements') ||
  1237→                linkText.includes('Setup Steps') ||
  1238→                linkText.includes('OpenAI Setup') ||
  1239→                linkText.includes('Anthropic Claude Setup') ||
  1240→                linkText.includes('Testing Your Setup') ||
  1241→                linkText.includes('Local LLM Options')) {
  1242→                const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
  1243→                if (listItem) {
  1244→                    console.log('Showing public nav item:', linkText);
  1245→                    listItem.style.display = '';
  1246→                }
  1247→            }
  1248→        });
  1249→    }
  1250→
  1251→    // REMOVED: MutationObserver navigation interference
  1252→    // Let MkDocs handle navigation structure completely
  1253→    // Content visibility is handled by CSS classes only

  "old_string": "    // Initialize when DOM is ready and on every page load\n    function runDetection() {\n        // Prevent multiple simultaneous detections\n        if (detectionInProgress) {\n            console.log('🔄 Detection already in progress, skipping...');\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        // Clear any pending detection\n        if (detectionTimeout) {\n            clearTimeout(detectionTimeout);\n        }\n        \n        // Debounce detection to prevent rapid successive calls\n        detectionTimeout = setTimeout(() => {\n            if (detectionInProgress) return;\n            \n            detectionInProgress = true;\n            console.log('🔄 Starting fresh network detection...');\n            \n            // Clean up navigation state first\n            cleanupNavigationState();\n            \n            try {\n                initializeNetworkDetection();\n            } finally {\n                // Reset detection flag after a delay to allow for async operations\n                setTimeout(() => {\n                    detectionInProgress = false;\n                }, 2000);\n            }\n        }, 100);\n    }",
  "new_string": "    // Initialize when DOM is ready and on every page load\n    function runDetection() {\n        // Prevent multiple simultaneous detections\n        if (detectionInProgress) {\n            console.log('🔄 Detection already in progress, skipping...');\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        // Clear any pending detection\n        if (detectionTimeout) {\n            clearTimeout(detectionTimeout);\n        }\n        \n        // More aggressive debounce detection to prevent rapid successive calls\n        detectionTimeout = setTimeout(() => {\n            if (detectionInProgress) return;\n            \n            detectionInProgress = true;\n            console.log('🔄 Starting fresh network detection...');\n            \n            // Clean up navigation state first\n            cleanupNavigationState();\n            \n            try {\n                initializeNetworkDetection();\n            } finally {\n                // Reset detection flag after longer delay to prevent rapid re-runs\n                setTimeout(() => {\n                    detectionInProgress = false;\n                    console.log('✅ Network detection cycle complete, ready for next run');\n                }, 5000); // Increased from 2000 to 5000ms\n            }\n        }, 300); // Increased from 100 to 300ms debounce delay\n    }"
}

   477→    // Initialize when DOM is ready and on every page load
   478→    function runDetection() {
   479→        // Prevent multiple simultaneous detections
   480→        if (detectionInProgress) {
   481→            console.log('🔄 Detection already in progress, skipping...');
   482→            return;
   483→        }
   484→        
   485→        // Clear any pending detection
   486→        if (detectionTimeout) {
   487→            clearTimeout(detectionTimeout);
   488→        }
   489→        
   490→        // More aggressive debounce detection to prevent rapid successive calls
   491→        detectionTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
   492→            if (detectionInProgress) return;
   493→            
   494→            detectionInProgress = true;
   495→            console.log('🔄 Starting fresh network detection...');
   496→            
   497→            // Clean up navigation state first
   498→            cleanupNavigationState();
   499→            
   500→            try {
   501→                initializeNetworkDetection();
   502→            } finally {
   503→                // Reset detection flag after longer delay to prevent rapid re-runs
   504→                setTimeout(() => {
   505→                    detectionInProgress = false;
   506→                    console.log('✅ Network detection cycle complete, ready for next run');
   507→                }, 5000); // Increased from 2000 to 5000ms
   508→            }
   509→        }, 300); // Increased from 100 to 300ms debounce delay
   510→    }
   511→    
   512→    // Initial run
   513→    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
   514→        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', runDetection);

     1→# Agent Frameworks Module
     2→
     3→Welcome to the **Agent Frameworks** module of the Agentic AI Nano-Degree! In the rapidly evolving landscape of AI-powered systems, the ability to architect, deploy, and scale intelligent agents has become a critical competitive advantage. This comprehensive 10-session journey transforms you from understanding basic agent concepts to building production-ready distributed systems that can handle real-world complexity and scale.
     4→
     5→![Agentic AI](images/agentic-ai.png)
     6→*Agents use LLMs to process natural language - this makes them integrate well with complex and human centric workflows*
     7→
     8→## Module Overview
     9→
    10→The modern software engineering landscape is experiencing a paradigm shift. Traditional applications are becoming intelligent, and data pipelines are evolving into autonomous systems capable of reasoning, planning, and executing complex tasks. This module covers the complete landscape of modern AI agent development, focusing on practical frameworks, patterns, and production deployment strategies that data engineers and system architects need to build reliable, scalable agent-driven solutions.
    11→
    12→**Duration**: 10 Sessions
    13→**Time Investment**: 60-180 minutes per session (depending on chosen path)
    14→**Prerequisites**: Intermediate Python, basic ML concepts
    15→
    16→## Learning Journey
    17→
    18→### Foundation (Sessions 0-2)
    19→
    20→Every production-ready system starts with solid fundamentals. These opening sessions establish the conceptual foundation you'll build upon throughout your agent development career, covering the architectural decisions that separate toy implementations from enterprise-grade solutions.
    21→
    22→### Session 0: Introduction to Agent Frameworks & Patterns
    23→
    24→Understanding the landscape is crucial before choosing your tools. This session provides the strategic foundation for making informed architectural decisions.
    25→
    26→- Agent architecture fundamentals

    29→- Historical context and evolution  
    30→

    32→

    34→
